34→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/pkg/v3/pbutil\"\n    35→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/config\"\n    36→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/etcdserver/api\"\n    37→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/etcdserver/api/membership\"\n    38→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/etcdserver/api/rafthttp\"\n    39→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/etcdserver/api/snap\"\n    40→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/etcdserver/api/v3discovery\"\n    41→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/etcdserver/cindex\"\n    42→\tservererrors \"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/etcdserver/errors\"\n    43→\tserverstorage \"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/storage\"\n    44→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/storage/backend\"\n    45→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/storage/schema\"\n    46→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/storage/wal\"\n    47→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/storage/wal/walpb\"\n    48→\t\"go.etcd.io/raft/v3\"\n    49→\t\"go.etcd.io/raft/v3/raftpb\"\n    50→)\n    51→\n    52→func bootstrap(cfg config.ServerConfig) (b *bootstrappedServer, err error) {\n    53→\tif cfg.MaxRequestBytes > recommendedMaxRequestBytes {\n    54→\t\tcfg.Logger.Warn(\n    55→\t\t\t\"exceeded recommended request limit\",\n    56→\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"max-request-bytes\", cfg.MaxRequestBytes),\n    57→\t\t\tzap.String(\"max-request-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(cfg.MaxRequestBytes))),\n    58→\t\t\tzap.Int(\"recommended-request-bytes\", recommendedMaxRequestBytes),\n    59→\t\t\tzap.String(\"recommended-request-size\", recommendedMaxRequestBytesString),\n    60→\t\t)\n    61→\t}\n    62→\n    63→\tif terr := fileutil.TouchDirAll(cfg.Logger, cfg.DataDir); terr != nil {\n    64→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot access data directory: %w\", terr)\n    65→\t}\n    66→\n    67→\tif terr := fileutil.TouchDirAll(cfg.Logger, cfg.MemberDir()); terr != nil {\n    68→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot access member directory: %w\", terr)\n    69→\t}\n    70→\tss := bootstrapSnapshot(cfg)\n    71→\tprt, err := rafthttp.NewRoundTripper(cfg.PeerTLSInfo, cfg.PeerDialTimeout())\n    72→\tif err != nil {\n    73→\t\treturn nil, err\n    74→\t}\n    75→\n    76→\thaveWAL := wal.Exist(cfg.WALDir())\n    77→\tbackend, err := bootstrapBackend(cfg, haveWAL)\n    78→\tif err != nil {\n    79→\t\treturn nil, err\n    80→\t}\n    81→\tvar bwal *bootstrappedWAL\n    82→\n    83→\tif haveWAL {\n    84→\t\tif err = fileutil.IsDirWriteable(cfg.WALDir()); err != nil {\n    85→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot write to WAL directory: %w\", err)\n    86→\t\t}\n    87→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Bootstrapping WAL from snapshot\")\n    88→\t\tbwal = bootstrapWALFromSnapshot(cfg, backend.snapshot, backend.ci)\n    89→\t}\n    90→\n    91→\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"bootstrapping cluster\")\n    92→\tcluster, err := bootstrapCluster(cfg, bwal, prt)\n    93→\tif err != nil {\n    94→\t\tbackend.Close()\n    95→\t\treturn nil, err\n    96→\t}\n    97→\n    98→\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"bootstrapping storage\")\n    99→\ts := bootstrapStorage(cfg, backend, bwal, cluster)\n   100→\n   101→\tif err = cluster.Finalize(cfg, s); err != nil {\n   102→\t\tbackend.Close()\n   103→\t\treturn nil, err\n   104→\t}\n   105→\n   106→\tif haveWAL {\n   107→\t\tsn := s.wal.snapshot\n   108→\t\tif sn == nil {\n   109→\t\t\tsn = &raftpb.Snapshot{}\n   110→\t\t}\n   111→\t\tcs := buildConfStateFromV3store(cfg.Logger, backend.be)\n   112→\n   113→\t\tsn.Metadata.ConfState = cs\n   114→\t\ts.wal.snapshot = sn\n   115→\n   116→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Constructed a new raft snapshot from v3 state\", zap.Uint64(\"index\", sn.Metadata.Index),\n   117→\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"term\", sn.Metadata.Term), zap.String(\"confState\", sn.Metadata.ConfState.String()))\n   118→\t}\n   119→\n   120→\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"bootstrapping raft\")\n   121→\traft := bootstrapRaft(cfg, cluster, s.wal)\n   122→\treturn &bootstrappedServer{\n   123→\t\tprt:     prt,\n   124→\t\tss:      ss,\n   125→\t\tstorage: s,\n   126→\t\tcluster: cluster,\n   127→\t\traft:    raft,\n   128→\t}, nil\n   129→}\n   130→\n   131→func buildConfStateFromV3store(lg *zap.Logger, be backend.Backend) raftpb.ConfState {\n   132→\tmembers, _ := schema.NewMembershipBackend(lg, be).MustReadMembersFromBackend()\n   133→\tvar (\n   134→\t\tvoters   []uint64\n   135→\t\tlearners []uint64\n   136→\t)\n   137→\tfor _, m := range members {\n   138→\t\tif m.IsLearner {\n   139→\t\t\tlearners = append(learners, uint64(m.ID))\n   140→\t\t} else {\n   141→\t\t\tvoters = append(voters, uint64(m.ID))\n   142→\t\t}\n   143→\t}\n   144→\treturn raftpb.ConfState{\n   145→\t\tVoters:   voters,\n   146→\t\tLearners: learners,\n   147→\t}\n   148→}\n   149→\n   150→type bootstrappedServer struct {\n   151→\tstorage *bootstrappedStorage\n   152→\tcluster *bootstrappedCluster\n   153→\traft    *bootstrappedRaft\n   154→\tprt     http.RoundTripper\n   155→\tss      *snap.Snapshotter\n   156→}\n   157→\n   158→func (s *bootstrappedServer) Close() {\n   159→\ts.storage.Close()\n   160→}\n   161→\n   162→type bootstrappedStorage struct {\n   163→\tbackend *bootstrappedBackend\n   164→\twal     *bootstrappedWAL\n   165→}\n   166→\n   167→func (s *bootstrappedStorage) Close() {\n   168→\ts.backend.Close()\n   169→}\n   170→\n   171→type bootstrappedBackend struct {\n   172→\tbeHooks  *serverstorage.BackendHooks\n   173→\tbe       backend.Backend\n   174→\tci       cindex.ConsistentIndexer\n   175→\tbeExist  bool\n   176→\tsnapshot *raftpb.Snapshot\n   177→}\n   178→\n   179→func (s *bootstrappedBackend) Close() {\n   180→\ts.be.Close()\n   181→}\n   182→\n   183→type bootstrappedCluster struct {\n   184→\tremotes []*membership.Member\n   185→\tcl      *membership.RaftCluster\n   186→\tnodeID  types.ID\n   187→}\n   188→\n   189→type bootstrappedRaft struct {\n   190→\tlg        *zap.Logger\n   191→\theartbeat time.Duration\n   192→\n   193→\tpeers   []raft.Peer\n   194→\tconfig  *raft.Config\n   195→\tstorage *raft.MemoryStorage\n   196→}\n   197→\n   198→func bootstrapStorage(cfg config.ServerConfig, be *bootstrappedBackend, wal *bootstrappedWAL, cl *bootstrappedCluster) *bootstrappedStorage {\n   199→\tif wal == nil {\n   200→\t\twal = bootstrapNewWAL(cfg, cl)\n   201→\t}\n   202→\n   203→\treturn &bootstrappedStorage{\n   204→\t\tbackend: be,\n   205→\t\twal:     wal,\n   206→\t}\n   207→}\n   208→\n   209→func bootstrapSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig) *snap.Snapshotter {\n   210→\tif err := fileutil.TouchDirAll(cfg.Logger, cfg.SnapDir()); err != nil {\n   211→\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\n   212→\t\t\t\"failed to create snapshot directory\",\n   213→\t\t\tzap.String(\"path\", cfg.SnapDir()),\n   214→\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n   215→\t\t)\n   216→\t}\n   217→\n   218→\tif err := fileutil.RemoveMatchFile(cfg.Logger, cfg.SnapDir(), func(fileName string) bool {\n   219→\t\treturn strings.HasPrefix(fileName, \"tmp\")\n   220→\t}); err != nil {\n   221→\t\tcfg.Logger.Error(\n   222→\t\t\t\"failed to remove temp file(s) in snapshot directory\",\n   223→\t\t\tzap.String(\"path\", cfg.SnapDir()),\n   224→\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n   225→\t\t)\n   226→\t}\n   227→\treturn snap.New(cfg.Logger, cfg.SnapDir())\n   228→}\n   229→\n   230→func bootstrapBackend(cfg config.ServerConfig, haveWAL bool) (backend *bootstrappedBackend, err error) {\n   231→\tbeExist := fileutil.Exist(cfg.BackendPath())\n   232→\tci := cindex.NewConsistentIndex(nil)\n   233→\tbeHooks := serverstorage.NewBackendHooks(cfg.Logger, ci)\n   234→\tbe := serverstorage.OpenBackend(cfg, beHooks)\n   235→\tdefer func() {\n   236→\t\tif err != nil && be != nil {\n   237→\t\t\tbe.Close()\n   238→\t\t}\n   239→\t}()\n   240→\tci.SetBackend(be)\n   241→\tschema.CreateMetaBucket(be.BatchTx())\n   242→\tif cfg.BootstrapDefragThresholdMegabytes != 0 {\n   243→\t\terr = maybeDefragBackend(cfg, be)\n   244→\t\tif err != nil {\n   245→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   246→\t\t}\n   247→\t}\n   248→\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"restore consistentIndex\", zap.Uint64(\"index\", ci.ConsistentIndex()))\n   249→\n   250→\t// TODO(serathius): Implement schema setup in fresh storage\n   251→\tvar snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot\n   252→\tif haveWAL {\n   253→\t\tsnapshot, be, err = recoverSnapshot(cfg, be, beExist, beHooks, ci)\n   254→\t\tif err != nil {\n   255→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   256→\t\t}\n   257→\t}\n   258→\tif beExist {\n   259→\t\ts1, s2 := be.Size(), be.SizeInUse()\n   260→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n   261→\t\t\t\"recovered v3 backend\",\n   262→\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"backend-size-bytes\", s1),\n   263→\t\t\tzap.String(\"backend-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(s1))),\n   264→\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"backend-size-in-use-bytes\", s2),\n   265→\t\t\tzap.String(\"backend-size-in-use\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(s2))),\n   266→\t\t)\n   267→\t\tif err = schema.Validate(cfg.Logger, be.ReadTx()); err != nil {\n   268→\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Error(\"Failed to validate schema\", zap.Error(err))\n   269→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   270→\t\t}\n   271→\t}\n   272→\n   273→\treturn &bootstrappedBackend{\n   274→\t\tbeHooks:  beHooks,\n   275→\t\tbe:       be,\n   276→\t\tci:       ci,\n   277→\t\tbeExist:  beExist,\n   278→\t\tsnapshot: snapshot,\n   279→\t}, nil\n   280→}\n   281→\n   282→func maybeDefragBackend(cfg config.ServerConfig, be backend.Backend) error {\n   283→\tsize := be.Size()\n   284→\tsizeInUse := be.SizeInUse()\n   285→\tfreeableMemory := uint(size - sizeInUse)\n   286→\tthresholdBytes := cfg.BootstrapDefragThresholdMegabytes * 1024 * 1024\n   287→\tif freeableMemory < thresholdBytes {\n   288→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Skipping defragmentation\",\n   289→\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"current-db-size-bytes\", size),\n   290→\t\t\tzap.String(\"current-db-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(size))),\n   291→\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"current-db-size-in-use-bytes\", sizeInUse),\n   292→\t\t\tzap.String(\"current-db-size-in-use\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(sizeInUse))),\n   293→\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"bootstrap-defrag-threshold-bytes\", thresholdBytes),\n   294→\t\t\tzap.String(\"bootstrap-defrag-threshold\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(thresholdBytes))),\n   295→\t\t)\n   296→\t\treturn nil\n   297→\t}\n   298→\treturn be.Defrag()\n   299→}\n   300→\n   301→func bootstrapCluster(cfg config.ServerConfig, bwal *bootstrappedWAL, prt http.RoundTripper) (c *bootstrappedCluster, err error) {\n   302→\tswitch {\n   303→\tcase bwal == nil && !cfg.NewCluster:\n   304→\t\tc, err = bootstrapExistingClusterNoWAL(cfg, prt)\n   305→\tcase bwal == nil && cfg.NewCluster:\n   306→\t\tc, err = bootstrapNewClusterNoWAL(cfg, prt)\n   307→\tcase bwal != nil && bwal.haveWAL:\n   308→\t\tc, err = bootstrapClusterWithWAL(cfg, bwal.meta)\n   309→\tdefault:\n   310→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported bootstrap config\")\n   311→\t}\n   312→\tif err != nil {\n   313→\t\treturn nil, err\n   314→\t}\n   315→\treturn c, nil\n   316→}\n   317→\n   318→func bootstrapExistingClusterNoWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, prt http.RoundTripper) (*bootstrappedCluster, error) {\n   319→\tif err := cfg.VerifyJoinExisting(); err != nil {\n   320→\t\treturn nil, err\n   321→\t}\n   322→\tcl, err := membership.NewClusterFromURLsMap(cfg.Logger, cfg.InitialClusterToken, cfg.InitialPeerURLsMap, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners))\n   323→\tif err != nil {\n   324→\t\treturn nil, err\n   325→\t}\n   326→\texistingCluster, gerr := GetClusterFromRemotePeers(cfg.Logger, getRemotePeerURLs(cl, cfg.Name), prt)\n   327→\tif gerr != nil {\n   328→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot fetch cluster info from peer urls: %w\", gerr)\n   329→\t}\n   330→\tif err := membership.ValidateClusterAndAssignIDs(cfg.Logger, cl, existingCluster); err != nil {\n   331→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error validating peerURLs %s: %w\", existingCluster, err)\n   332→\t}\n   333→\tif !isCompatibleWithCluster(cfg.Logger, cl, cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name).ID, prt, cfg.ReqTimeout()) {\n   334→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"incompatible with current running cluster\")\n   335→\t}\n   336→\tscaleUpLearners := false\n   337→\tif err := membership.ValidateMaxLearnerConfig(cfg.MaxLearners, existingCluster.Members(), scaleUpLearners); err != nil {\n   338→\t\treturn nil, err\n   339→\t}\n   340→\tremotes := existingCluster.Members()\n   341→\tcl.SetID(types.ID(0), existingCluster.ID())\n   342→\tmember := cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name)\n   343→\treturn &bootstrappedCluster{\n   344→\t\tremotes: remotes,\n   345→\t\tcl:      cl,\n   346→\t\tnodeID:  member.ID,\n   347→\t}, nil\n   348→}\n   349→\n   350→func bootstrapNewClusterNoWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, prt http.RoundTripper) (*bootstrappedCluster, error) {\n   351→\tif err := cfg.VerifyBootstrap(); err != nil {\n   352→\t\treturn nil, err\n   353→\t}\n   354→\tcl, err := membership.NewClusterFromURLsMap(cfg.Logger, cfg.InitialClusterToken, cfg.InitialPeerURLsMap, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners))\n   355→\tif err != nil {\n   356→\t\treturn nil, err\n   357→\t}\n   358→\tm := cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name)\n   359→\tif isMemberBootstrapped(cfg.Logger, cl, cfg.Name, prt, cfg.BootstrapTimeoutEffective()) {\n   360→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"member %s has already been bootstrapped\", m.ID)\n   361→\t}\n   362→\tif cfg.ShouldDiscover() {\n   363→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Bootstrapping cluster using v3 discovery.\")\n   364→\t\tstr, err := v3discovery.JoinCluster(cfg.Logger, &cfg.DiscoveryCfg, m.ID, cfg.InitialPeerURLsMap.String())\n   365→\t\tif err != nil {\n   366→\t\t\treturn nil, &servererrors.DiscoveryError{Op: \"join\", Err: err}\n   367→\t\t}\n   368→\t\tvar urlsmap types.URLsMap\n   369→\t\turlsmap, err = types.NewURLsMap(str)\n   370→\t\tif err != nil {\n   371→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   372→\t\t}\n   373→\t\tif config.CheckDuplicateURL(urlsmap) {\n   374→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"discovery cluster %s has duplicate url\", urlsmap)\n   375→\t\t}\n   376→\t\tif cl, err = membership.NewClusterFromURLsMap(cfg.Logger, cfg.InitialClusterToken, urlsmap, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners)); err != nil {\n   377→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   378→\t\t}\n   379→\t}\n   380→\treturn &bootstrappedCluster{\n   381→\t\tremotes: nil,\n   382→\t\tcl:      cl,\n   383→\t\tnodeID:  m.ID,\n   384→\t}, nil\n   385→}\n   386→\n   387→func bootstrapClusterWithWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, meta *snapshotMetadata) (*bootstrappedCluster, error) {\n   388→\tif err := fileutil.IsDirWriteable(cfg.MemberDir()); err != nil {\n   389→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot write to member directory: %w\", err)\n   390→\t}\n   391→\n   392→\tif cfg.ShouldDiscover() {\n   393→\t\tcfg.Logger.Warn(\n   394→\t\t\t\"discovery token is ignored since cluster already initialized; valid logs are found\",\n   395→\t\t\tzap.String(\"wal-dir\", cfg.WALDir()),\n   396→\t\t)\n   397→\t}\n   398→\tcl := membership.NewCluster(cfg.Logger, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners))\n   399→\n   400→\tscaleUpLearners := false\n   401→\tif err := membership.ValidateMaxLearnerConfig(cfg.MaxLearners, cl.Members(), scaleUpLearners); err != nil {\n   402→\t\treturn nil, err\n   403→\t}\n   404→\n   405→\tcl.SetID(meta.nodeID, meta.clusterID)\n   406→\treturn &bootstrappedCluster{\n   407→\t\tcl:     cl,\n   408→\t\tnodeID: meta.nodeID,\n   409→\t}, nil\n   410→}\n   411→\n   412→func recoverSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig, be backend.Backend, beExist bool, beHooks *serverstorage.BackendHooks, ci cindex.ConsistentIndexer) (*raftpb.Snapshot, backend.Backend, error) {\n   413→\t// Find a snapshot to start/restart a raft node\n   414→\twalSnaps, err := wal.ValidSnapshotEntries(cfg.Logger, cfg.WALDir())\n   415→\tif err != nil {\n   416→\t\treturn nil, be, err\n   417→\t}\n   418→\n   419→\tvar snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot\n   420→\tif len(walSnaps) > 0 {\n   421→\t\tidx := len(walSnaps) - 1\n   422→\t\tsnapshot = &raftpb.Snapshot{\n   423→\t\t\tMetadata: raftpb.SnapshotMetadata{\n   424→\t\t\t\tTerm:  walSnaps[idx].Term,\n   425→\t\t\t\tIndex: walSnaps[idx].Index,\n   426→\t\t\t},\n   427→\t\t}\n   428→\t\tif walSnaps[idx].ConfState != nil {\n   429→\t\t\tsnapshot.Metadata.ConfState = *walSnaps[idx].ConfState\n   430→\t\t}\n   431→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"constructed a snapshot from WAL record\",\n   432→\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"snapshot-index\", snapshot.Metadata.Index),\n   433→\t\t\tzap.String(\"snapshot-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(snapshot.Size()))),\n   434→\t\t\tzap.String(\"confState\", snapshot.Metadata.ConfState.String()),\n   435→\t\t\tzap.Int(\"walSnaps-count\", len(walSnaps)),\n   436→\t\t)\n   437→\t}\n   438→\n   439→\tif snapshot != nil {\n   440→\t\tif be, err = serverstorage.RecoverSnapshotBackend(cfg, be, *snapshot, beExist, beHooks); err != nil {\n   441→\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Panic(\"failed to recover v3 backend from snapshot\", zap.Error(err))\n   442→\t\t}\n   443→\t\t// A snapshot db may have already been recovered, and the old db should have\n   444→\t\t// already been closed in this case, so we should set the backend again.\n   445→\t\tci.SetBackend(be)\n   446→\n   447→\t\tif beExist {\n   448→\t\t\t// TODO: remove kvindex != 0 checking when we do not expect users to upgrade\n   449→\t\t\t// etcd from pre-3.0 release.\n   450→\t\t\tkvindex := ci.ConsistentIndex()\n   451→\t\t\tif kvindex < snapshot.Metadata.Index {\n   452→\t\t\t\tif kvindex != 0 {\n   453→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, be, fmt.Errorf(\"database file (%v index %d) does not match with snapshot (index %d)\", cfg.BackendPath(), kvindex, snapshot.Metadata.Index)\n   454→\t\t\t\t}\n   455→\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Warn(\n   456→\t\t\t\t\t\"consistent index was never saved\",\n   457→\t\t\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"snapshot-index\", snapshot.Metadata.Index),\n   458→\t\t\t\t)\n   459→\t\t\t}\n   460→\t\t}\n   461→\t} else {\n   462→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"No snapshot found. Recovering WAL from scratch!\")\n   463→\t}\n   464→\treturn snapshot, be, nil\n   465→}\n   466→\n   467→func (c *bootstrappedCluster) Finalize(cfg config.ServerConfig, s *bootstrappedStorage) error {\n   468→\tif !s.wal.haveWAL {\n   469→\t\tc.cl.SetID(c.nodeID, c.cl.ID())\n   470→\t}\n   471→\tc.cl.SetBackend(schema.NewMembershipBackend(cfg.Logger, s.backend.be))\n   472→\tif s.wal.haveWAL {\n   473→\t\tc.cl.Recover(api.UpdateCapability)\n   474→\t\tif c.databaseFileMissing(s) {\n   475→\t\t\tbepath := cfg.BackendPath()\n   476→\t\t\tos.RemoveAll(bepath)\n   477→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"database file (%v) of the backend is missing\", bepath)\n   478→\t\t}\n   479→\t}\n   480→\tscaleUpLearners := false\n   481→\treturn membership.ValidateMaxLearnerConfig(cfg.MaxLearners, c.cl.Members(), scaleUpLearners)\n   482→}\n   483→\n   484→func (c *bootstrappedCluster) databaseFileMissing(s *bootstrappedStorage) bool {\n   485→\tv3Cluster := c.cl.Version() != nil && !c.cl.Version().LessThan(semver.Version{Major: 3})\n   486→\treturn v3Cluster && !s.backend.beExist\n   487→}\n   488→\n   489→func bootstrapRaft(cfg config.ServerConfig, cluster *bootstrappedCluster, bwal *bootstrappedWAL) *bootstrappedRaft {\n   490→\tswitch {\n   491→\tcase !bwal.haveWAL && !cfg.NewCluster:\n   492→\t\treturn bootstrapRaftFromCluster(cfg, cluster.cl, nil, bwal)\n   493→\tcase !bwal.haveWAL && cfg.NewCluster:\n   494→\t\treturn bootstrapRaftFromCluster(cfg, cluster.cl, cluster.cl.MemberIDs(), bwal)\n   495→\tcase bwal.haveWAL:\n   496→\t\treturn bootstrapRaftFromWAL(cfg, bwal)\n   497→\tdefault:\n   498→\t\tcfg.Logger.Panic(\"unsupported bootstrap config\")\n   499→\t\treturn nil\n   500→\t}\n   501→}\n   502→\n   503→func bootstrapRaftFromCluster(cfg config.ServerConfig, cl *membership.RaftCluster, ids []types.ID, bwal *bootstrappedWAL) *bootstrappedRaft {\n   504→\tmember := cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name)\n   505→\tpeers := make([]raft.Peer, 524→\t\tpeers:     peers,\n   525→\t\tstorage:   s,\n   526→\t}\n   527→}\n   528→\n   529→func bootstrapRaftFromWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, bwal *bootstrappedWAL) *bootstrappedRaft {\n   530→\ts := bwal.MemoryStorage()\n   531→\treturn &bootstrappedRaft{\n   532→\t\tlg:        cfg.Logger,\n   533→\t\theartbeat: time.Duration(cfg.TickMs) * time.Millisecond,\n   534→\t\tconfig:    raftConfig(cfg, NewRaftLoggerZap(cfg.Logger.Named(\"raft\")),\n   550→\t}\n   551→}\n   552→\n   553→func (b *bootstrappedRaft) newRaftNode(ss *snap.Snapshotter, wal *wal.WAL, cl *membership.RaftCluster) *raftNode {\n   554→\tvar n raft.Node\n   555→\tif len(b.peers) == 0 {\n   556→\t\tn = raft.RestartNode(b.config)\n   557→\t} else {\n   558→\t\tn = raft.StartNode(b.config, b.peers)\n   559→\t}\n 570→\t\t\tstorage:     serverstorage.NewStorage(b.lg, wal, ss),\n   571→\t\t},\n   572→\t)\n   573→}\n   574→\n   575→func bootstrapWALFromSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig, snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot, ci cindex.ConsistentIndexer) *bootstrappedWAL {\n   576→\twal, st, ents, snap, meta := openWALFromSnapshot(cfg, snapshot)\n   577→\tbwal := &bootstrappedWAL{\n   578→\t\tlg:       cfg.Logger,\n   579→\t\tw:        wal,\n   580→\t\tst:       st,\n   581→\t\tents:     ents,\n   582→\t\tsnapshot: snap,\n   583→\t\tmeta:     meta,\n   584→\t\thaveWAL:  true,\n   585→\t}\n   586→\n   587→\tif cfg.ForceNewCluster {\n   588→\t\tconsistentIndex := ci.ConsistentIndex()\n   589→\t\toldCommitIndex := bwal.st.Commit\n   590→\t\t// If only `HardState.Commit` increases, HardState won't be persisted\n   591→\t\t// to disk, even though the committed entries might have already been\n   592→\t\t// applied. This can result in consistent_index > CommitIndex.\n   593→\t\t//\n   594→\t\t// When restarting etcd with `--force-new-cluster`, all uncommitted\n   595→\t\t// entries are dropped. To avoid losing entries that were actually\n   596→\t\t// committed, we reset Commit to max(HardState.Commit, consistent_index).\n   597→\t\t//\n   598→\t\t// See: https://github.com/etcd-io/raft/pull/300 for more details.\n   599→\t\tbwal.st.Commit = max(oldCommitIndex, consistentIndex)\n   600→\n   601→\t\t// discard the previously uncommitted entries\n   602→\t\tbwal.ents = bwal.CommitedEntries()\n   603→\t\tentries := bwal.NewConfigChangeEntries()\n   604→\t\t// force commit config change entries\n   605→\t\tbwal.AppendAndCommitEntries(entries)\n   606→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n   607→\t\t\t\"forcing restart member\",\n   608→\t\t\tzap.String(\"cluster-id\", meta.clusterID.String()),\n   609→\t\t\tzap.String(\"local-member-id\", meta.nodeID.String()),\n   610→\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"wal-commit-index\", oldCommitIndex),\n   611→\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"commit-index\", bwal.st.Commit),\n   612→\t\t)\n   613→\t} else {\n   614→\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n   615→\t\t\t\"restarting local member\",\n   616→\t\t\tzap.String(\"cluster-id\", meta.clusterID.String()),\n   617→\t\t\tzap.String(\"local-member-id\", meta.nodeID.String()),\n   618→\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"commit-index\", bwal.st.Commit),\n   619→\t\t)\n   620→\t}\n   621→\treturn bwal\n   622→}\n   623→\n   624→// openWALFromSnapshot reads the WAL at the given snap and returns the wal, its latest HardState and cluster ID, and all entries that appear\n   625→// after the position of the given snap in the WAL.\n   626→// The snap must have been previously saved to the WAL, or this call will panic.\n   627→func openWALFromSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig, snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot) (*wal.WAL, *raftpb.HardState, []raftpb.Entry, *raftpb.Snapshot, *snapshotMetadata) {\n   628→\tvar walsnap walpb.Snapshot\n   629→\tif snapshot != nil {\n   630→\t\twalsnap.Index, walsnap.Term = snapshot.Metadata.Index, snapshot.Metadata.Term\n   631→\t}\n   632→\trepaired := false\n   633→\tfor {\n   634→\t\tw, err := wal.Open(cfg.Logger, cfg.WALDir(), walsnap)\n   635→\t\tif err != nil {\n   636→\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\"failed to open WAL\", zap.Error(err))\n   637→\t\t}\n   638→\t\tif cfg.UnsafeNoFsync {\n   639→\t\t\tw.SetUnsafeNoFsync()\n   640→\t\t}\n   641→\t\twmetadata, st, ents, err := w.ReadAll()\n   642→\t\tif err != nil {\n   643→\t\t\tw.Close()\n   644→\t\t\t// we can only repair ErrUnexpectedEOF and we never repair twice.\n   645→\t\t\tif repaired || !errors.Is(err, io.ErrUnexpectedEOF) {\n   646→\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\"failed to read WAL, cannot be repaired\", zap.Error(err))\n   647→\t\t\t}\n   648→\t\t\tif !wal.Repair(cfg.Logger, cfg.WALDir()) {\n   649→\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\"failed to repair WAL\", zap.Error(err))\n   650→\t\t\t} else {\n   651→\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"repaired WAL\", zap.Error(err))\n   652→\t\t\t\trepaired = true\n   653→\t\t\t}\n   654→\t\t\tcontinue\n   655→\t\t}\n   656→\t\tvar metadata etcdserverpb.Metadata\n   657→\t\tpbutil.MustUnmarshal(&metadata, wmetadata)\n   658→\t\tid := types.ID(metadata.NodeID)\n   659→\t\tcid := types.ID(metadata.ClusterID)\n   660→\t\tmeta := &snapshotMetadata{clusterID: cid, nodeID: id}\n   661→\t\treturn w, &st, ents, snapshot, meta\n   662→\t}\n   663→}\n   664→\n   665→type snapshotMetadata struct {\n   666→\tnodeID, clusterID types.ID\n   667→}\n   668→\n   669→func bootstrapNewWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, cl *bootstrappedCluster) *bootstrappedWAL {\n 709→\t\ts.Append(wal.ents)\n   710→\t}\n   711→\treturn s\n   712→}\n   713→\n   714→func (wal *bootstrappedWAL) CommitedEntries() []raftpb.Entry {\n   715→\tfor i, ent := range wal.ents {\n   716→\t\tif ent.Index > wal.st.Commit {\n   717→\t\t\twal.lg.Info(\n   718→\t\t\t\t\"discarding uncommitted WAL entries\",\n   719→\t\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"entry-index\", ent.Index),\n 724→\t\t}\n   725→\t}\n   726→\treturn wal.ents\n   727→}\n   728→\n   729→func (wal *bootstrappedWAL) NewConfigChangeEntries() []raftpb.Entry {\n   730→\treturn bootstrap(cfg config.ServerConfig) (b *bootstrappedServer, err error) {\n\tif cfg.MaxRequestBytes > recommendedMaxRequestBytes {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Warn(\n\t\t\t\"exceeded recommended request limit\",\n\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"max-request-bytes\", cfg.MaxRequestBytes),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"max-request-size\", recommendedMaxRequestBytesString),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\tif terr := fileutil.TouchDirAll(cfg.Logger, cfg.DataDir); terr != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot access data directory: %w\", terr)\n\t}\n\n\tif terr := fileutil.TouchDirAll(cfg.Logger, cfg.MemberDir()); terr != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot access member directory: %w\", terr)\n\t}\n\tss := buildConfStateFromV3store(lg *zap.Logger, be backend.Backend) raftpb.ConfState {\n\tmembers, _ := schema.NewMembershipBackend(lg, be).MustReadMembersFromBackend()\n\tvar (\n\t\tvoters schema\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &bootstrappedBackend{\n\t\tbeHooks:  beHooks,\n\t\tbe:       be,\n\t\tci:       ci,\n\t\tbeExist:  beExist,\n\t\tsnapshot: snapshot,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc maybeDefragBackend(cfg config.ServerConfig, be backend.Backend) error {\n\tsize := be.Size()\n\tsizeInUse := be.SizeInUse()\n\tfreeableMemory := uint(size - sizeInUse)\n\tthresholdBytes := cfg.BootstrapDefragThresholdMegabytes * 1024 * 1024\n\tif freeableMemory < thresholdBytes {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Skipping defragmentation\",\n\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"current-db-size-bytes\", size),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"current-db-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(size))),\n\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"current-db-size-in-use-bytes\", sizeInUse),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"current-db-size-in-use\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(sizeInUse))),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"bootstrap-defrag-threshold-bytes\", uint64 = 10000\n\n// newRaftNode initiates a raft instance and returns a committed log entry\n// channel and error channel. Proposals for log updates are sent over the\n// provided the proposal channel. All log entries are replayed over the\n// commit channel, followed by a nil message (to indicate the channel is\n// current), then new log entries. To shutdown, close proposeC and read errorC.\nfunc newRaftNode(id int, peers []string, join bool, getSnapshot func() ([]byte, error), proposeC <-chan string,\n\tconfChangeC <-chan raftpb.ConfChange,\n) (<-chan *commit, <-chan error, <-chan *snap.Snapshotter) {\n\tcommitC := make(chan *commit)\n\terrorC := make(chan error)\n\n\trc := &raftNode{\n\t\tproposeC:    proposeC,\n\t\tconfChangeC: confChangeC,\n\t\tcommitC:     commitC,\n\t\terrorC:      errorC,\n\t\tid:          id,\n\t\tpeers:       peers,\n\t\tjoin:        join,\n\t\twaldir:      fmt.Sprintf(\"raftexample-%d\", id),\n\t\tsnapdir:     fmt.Sprintf(\"raftexample-%d-snap\", id),\n\t\tgetSnapshot: getSnapshot,\n\t\tsnapCount:   defaultSnapshotCount,\n\t\tstopc:       make(chan struct{}),\n\t\thttpstopc:   make(chan struct{}),\n\t\thttpdonec:   make(chan struct{}),\n\n\t\tlogger: zap.NewExample(),\n\n\t\tsnapshotterReady: make(chan *snap.Snapshotter, 1),\n\t\t// rest of structure populated after WAL replay\n\t}\n\tgo rc.startRaft()\n\treturn commitC, errorC, rc.snapshotterReady\n}\n\nfunc (rc *raftNode) saveSnap(snap raftpb.Snapshot) error {\n\twalSnap := walpb.Snapshot{\n\t\tIndex:     snap.Metadata.Index,\n\t\tTerm:      snap.Metadata.Term,\n\t\tConfState: &snap.Metadata.ConfState,\n\t}\n\t// save the snapshot file before writing the snapshot to the wal.\n\t// This makes it possible for the snapshot file to become orphaned, but prevents\n\t// a WAL snapshot entry from having no corresponding snapshot file.\n\tif err := rc.snapshotter.SaveSnap(snap); Shutting down.\")\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, false\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\trc.transport.RemovePeer(types.ID(cc.NodeID))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tvar applyDoneC chan struct{}\n\n\tif len(data) > 0 {\n\t\tapplyDoneC = make(chan struct{}, 1)\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase rc.commitC <- &commit{data, applyDoneC}:\n\t\tcase <-rc.stopc:\n\t\t\treturn nil, false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// after commit, update replayWAL() *wal.WAL {\n\tlog.Printf(\"replaying WAL of member %d\", rc.id)\n\tsnapshot := rc.loadSnapshot()\n\tw := rc.openWAL(snapshot)\n\t_, st, ents, err := w.ReadAll()\n\tif err != nil rc.snapCount {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// wait until all committed entries are applied (or server is closed)\n\tif applyDoneC != nil {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-applyDoneC:\n\t\tcase Proposals for log updates are sent over the\n// provided the proposal channel. All log entries are replayed over the\n// commit channel, followed by a nil message (to indicate the channel is\n// current), then new log entries. To shutdown, close proposeC and read errorC.\nfunc newRaftNode(id int, peers []string, join bool, getSnapshot func() ([]byte, error), proposeC <-chan string,\n\tconfChangeC <-chan raftpb.ConfChange,\n) (<-chan *commit, <-chan error, <-chan *snap.Snapshotter) {\n\tcommitC := make(chan *commit)\n\terrorC := make(chan error)\n\n\trc := &raftNode{\n\t\tproposeC:    proposeC,\n\t\tconfChangeC: confChangeC,\n\t\tcommitC:     commitC,\n\t\terrorC:      errorC,\n\t\tid:          id,\n\t\tpeers:       peers,\n\t\tjoin:        join,\n\t\twaldir:      fmt.Sprintf(\"raftexample-%d\", id),\n\t\tsnapdir:     fmt.Sprintf(\"raftexample-%d-snap\", id),\n\t\tgetSnapshot: getSnapshot,\n\t\tsnapCount:   defaultSnapshotCount,\n\t\tstopc:       make(chan struct{}),\n\t\thttpstopc:   make(chan struct{}),\n\t\thttpdonec:   make(chan struct{}),\n\n\t\tlogger: zap.NewExample(),\n\n\t\tsnapshotterReady: make(chan *snap.Snapshotter, 1),\n\t\t// rest of structure populated after WAL replay\n\t}\n\tgo rc.startRaft()\n\treturn commitC, errorC, rc.snapshotterReady\n}\n\nfunc (rc *raftNode) saveSnap(snap raftpb.Snapshot) error {\n\twalSnap := walpb.Snapshot{\n\t\tIndex:     snap.Metadata.Index,\n\t\tTerm:      snap.Metadata.Term,\n\t\tConfState: &snap.Metadata.ConfState,\n\t}\n\t// save the snapshot file before writing the snapshot to the wal.\n\t// This makes it possible for the snapshot file to become orphaned, but prevents\n\t// a WAL snapshot entry from having no corresponding snapshot file.\n\tif err := rc.snapshotter.SaveSnap(snap); err := bootstrapBackend(cfg, haveWAL)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tvar bwal *bootstrappedWAL\n\n\tif haveWAL {\n\t\tif err = fileutil.IsDirWriteable(cfg.WALDir()); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot write to WAL directory: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Bootstrapping WAL from snapshot\")\n\t\tbwal = bootstrapWALFromSnapshot(cfg, backend.snapshot, backend.ci)\n\t}\n\n\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"bootstrapping cluster\")\n\tcluster, err := bootstrapCluster(cfg, bwal, prt)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tbackend.Close()\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"bootstrapping storage\")\n\ts := bootstrapStorage(cfg, backend, bwal, cluster)\n\n\tif err = cluster.Finalize(cfg, s); err != nil {\n\t\tbackend.Close()\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif haveWAL {\n\t\tsn := s.wal.snapshot\n\t\tif sn == nil {\n\t\t\tsn = &raftpb.Snapshot{}\n\t\t}\n\t\tcs := buildConfStateFromV3store(cfg.Logger, backend.be)\n\n\t\tsn.Metadata.ConfState = cs\n\t\ts.wal.snapshot = sn\n\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Constructed a new raft snapshot from v3 state\", zap.Uint64(\"index\", sn.Metadata.Index),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"term\", sn.Metadata.Term), zap.String(\"confState\", sn.Metadata.ConfState.String()))\n\t}\n\n\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"bootstrapping raft\")\n\traft := bootstrapRaft(cfg, cluster, s.wal)\n\treturn &bootstrappedServer{\n\t\tprt:     prt,\n\t\tss:      ss,\n\t\tstorage: s,\n\t\tcluster: cluster,\n\t\traft:    raft,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc buildConfStateFromV3store(lg *zap.Logger, be backend.Backend) raftpb.ConfState {\n\tmembers, _ := schema.NewMembershipBackend(lg, be).MustReadMembersFromBackend()\n\tvar (\n\t\tvoters   []uint64\n\t\tlearners []uint64\n\t)\n\tfor _, m := range members {\n\t\tif m.IsLearner {\n\t\t\tlearners = append(learners, uint64(m.ID))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tvoters = append(voters, uint64(m.ID))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn raftpb.ConfState{\n\t\tVoters:   voters,\n\t\tLearners: learners,\n\t}\n}\n\ntype bootstrappedServer struct {\n\tstorage *bootstrappedStorage\n\tcluster *bootstrappedCluster\n\traft    *bootstrappedRaft\n\tprt     http.RoundTripper\n\tss      *snap.Snapshotter\n}\n\nfunc (s *bootstrappedServer) Close() {\n\ts.storage.Close()\n}\n\ntype bootstrappedStorage struct {\n\tbackend *bootstrappedBackend\n\twal     *bootstrappedWAL\n}\n\nfunc (s *bootstrappedStorage) Close() {\n\ts.backend.Close()\n}\n\ntype bootstrappedBackend struct {\n\tbeHooks  *serverstorage.BackendHooks\n\tbe       backend.Backend\n\tci       cindex.ConsistentIndexer\n\tbeExist  bool\n\tsnapshot *raftpb.Snapshot\n}\n\nfunc (s *bootstrappedBackend) Close() {\n\ts.be.Close()\n}\n\ntype bootstrappedCluster struct {\n\tremotes []*membership.Member\n\tcl      *membership.RaftCluster\n\tnodeID  types.ID\n}\n\ntype bootstrappedRaft struct {\n\tlg        *zap.Logger\n\theartbeat time.Duration\n\n\tpeers   []raft.Peer\n\tconfig  *raft.Config\n\tstorage *raft.MemoryStorage\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapStorage(cfg config.ServerConfig, be *bootstrappedBackend, wal *bootstrappedWAL, cl *bootstrappedCluster) *bootstrappedStorage {\n\tif wal == nil {\n\t\twal = bootstrapNewWAL(cfg, cl)\n\t}\n\n\treturn &bootstrappedStorage{\n\t\tbackend: be,\n\t\twal:     wal,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig) *snap.Snapshotter {\n\tif err := fileutil.TouchDirAll(cfg.Logger, cfg.SnapDir()); err != nil {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\n\t\t\t\"failed to create snapshot directory\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"path\", cfg.SnapDir()),\n\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\tif err := fileutil.RemoveMatchFile(cfg.Logger, cfg.SnapDir(), func(fileName string) bool {\n\t\treturn strings.HasPrefix(fileName, \"tmp\")\n\t}); err != nil {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Error(\n\t\t\t\"failed to remove temp file(s) in snapshot directory\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"path\", cfg.SnapDir()),\n\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn snap.New(cfg.Logger, cfg.SnapDir())\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapBackend(cfg config.ServerConfig, haveWAL bool) (backend *bootstrappedBackend, err error) {\n\tbeExist := fileutil.Exist(cfg.BackendPath())\n\tci := cindex.NewConsistentIndex(nil)\n\tbeHooks := serverstorage.NewBackendHooks(cfg.Logger, ci)\n\tbe := serverstorage.OpenBackend(cfg, beHooks)\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err != nil && be != nil {\n\t\t\tbe.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\tci.SetBackend(be)\n\tschema.CreateMetaBucket(be.BatchTx())\n\tif cfg.BootstrapDefragThresholdMegabytes != 0 {\n\t\terr = maybeDefragBackend(cfg, be)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"restore consistentIndex\", zap.Uint64(\"index\", ci.ConsistentIndex()))\n\n\t// TODO(serathius): Implement schema setup in fresh storage\n\tvar snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot\n\tif haveWAL {\n\t\tsnapshot, be, err = recoverSnapshot(cfg, be, beExist, beHooks, ci)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif beExist {\n\t\ts1, s2 := be.Size(), be.SizeInUse()\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\"recovered v3 backend\",\n\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"backend-size-bytes\", s1),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"backend-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(s1))),\n\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"backend-size-in-use-bytes\", s2),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"backend-size-in-use\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(s2))),\n\t\t)\n\t\tif err = schema.Validate(cfg.Logger, be.ReadTx()); err != nil {\n\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Error(\"Failed to validate schema\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &bootstrappedBackend{\n\t\tbeHooks:  beHooks,\n\t\tbe:       be,\n\t\tci:       ci,\n\t\tbeExist:  beExist,\n\t\tsnapshot: snapshot,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc maybeDefragBackend(cfg config.ServerConfig, be backend.Backend) error {\n\tsize := be.Size()\n\tsizeInUse := be.SizeInUse()\n\tfreeableMemory := uint(size - sizeInUse)\n\tthresholdBytes := cfg.BootstrapDefragThresholdMegabytes * 1024 * 1024\n\tif freeableMemory < thresholdBytes {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Skipping defragmentation\",\n\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"current-db-size-bytes\", size),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"current-db-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(size))),\n\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"current-db-size-in-use-bytes\", sizeInUse),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"current-db-size-in-use\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(sizeInUse))),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint(\"bootstrap-defrag-threshold-bytes\", thresholdBytes),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"bootstrap-defrag-threshold\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(thresholdBytes))),\n\t\t)\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\treturn be.Defrag()\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapCluster(cfg config.ServerConfig, bwal *bootstrappedWAL, prt http.RoundTripper) (c *bootstrappedCluster, err error) {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase bwal == nil && !cfg.NewCluster:\n\t\tc, err = bootstrapExistingClusterNoWAL(cfg, prt)\n\tcase bwal == nil && cfg.NewCluster:\n\t\tc, err = bootstrapNewClusterNoWAL(cfg, prt)\n\tcase bwal != nil && bwal.haveWAL:\n\t\tc, err = bootstrapClusterWithWAL(cfg, bwal.meta)\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported bootstrap config\")\n\t}\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn c, nil\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapExistingClusterNoWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, prt http.RoundTripper) (*bootstrappedCluster, error) {\n\tif err := cfg.VerifyJoinExisting(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tcl, err := membership.NewClusterFromURLsMap(cfg.Logger, cfg.InitialClusterToken, cfg.InitialPeerURLsMap, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\texistingCluster, gerr := GetClusterFromRemotePeers(cfg.Logger, getRemotePeerURLs(cl, cfg.Name), prt)\n\tif gerr != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot fetch cluster info from peer urls: %w\", gerr)\n\t}\n\tif err := membership.ValidateClusterAndAssignIDs(cfg.Logger, cl, existingCluster); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error validating peerURLs %s: %w\", existingCluster, err)\n\t}\n\tif !isCompatibleWithCluster(cfg.Logger, cl, cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name).ID, prt, cfg.ReqTimeout()) {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"incompatible with current running cluster\")\n\t}\n\tscaleUpLearners := false\n\tif err := membership.ValidateMaxLearnerConfig(cfg.MaxLearners, existingCluster.Members(), scaleUpLearners); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tremotes := existingCluster.Members()\n\tcl.SetID(types.ID(0), existingCluster.ID())\n\tmember := cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name)\n\treturn &bootstrappedCluster{\n\t\tremotes: remotes,\n\t\tcl:      cl,\n\t\tnodeID:  member.ID,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapNewClusterNoWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, prt http.RoundTripper) (*bootstrappedCluster, error) {\n\tif err := cfg.VerifyBootstrap(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tcl, err := membership.NewClusterFromURLsMap(cfg.Logger, cfg.InitialClusterToken, cfg.InitialPeerURLsMap, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tm := cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name)\n\tif isMemberBootstrapped(cfg.Logger, cl, cfg.Name, prt, cfg.BootstrapTimeoutEffective()) {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"member %s has already been bootstrapped\", m.ID)\n\t}\n\tif cfg.ShouldDiscover() {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"Bootstrapping cluster using v3 discovery.\")\n\t\tstr, err := v3discovery.JoinCluster(cfg.Logger, &cfg.DiscoveryCfg, m.ID, cfg.InitialPeerURLsMap.String())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, &servererrors.DiscoveryError{Op: \"join\", Err: err}\n\t\t}\n\t\tvar urlsmap types.URLsMap\n\t\turlsmap, err = types.NewURLsMap(str)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif config.CheckDuplicateURL(urlsmap) {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"discovery cluster %s has duplicate url\", urlsmap)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif cl, err = membership.NewClusterFromURLsMap(cfg.Logger, cfg.InitialClusterToken, urlsmap, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners)); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn &bootstrappedCluster{\n\t\tremotes: nil,\n\t\tcl:      cl,\n\t\tnodeID:  m.ID,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapClusterWithWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, meta *snapshotMetadata) (*bootstrappedCluster, error) {\n\tif err := fileutil.IsDirWriteable(cfg.MemberDir()); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot write to member directory: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tif cfg.ShouldDiscover() {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Warn(\n\t\t\t\"discovery token is ignored since cluster already initialized; valid logs are found\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"wal-dir\", cfg.WALDir()),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\tcl := membership.NewCluster(cfg.Logger, membership.WithMaxLearners(cfg.MaxLearners))\n\n\tscaleUpLearners := false\n\tif err := membership.ValidateMaxLearnerConfig(cfg.MaxLearners, cl.Members(), scaleUpLearners); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tcl.SetID(meta.nodeID, meta.clusterID)\n\treturn &bootstrappedCluster{\n\t\tcl:     cl,\n\t\tnodeID: meta.nodeID,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc recoverSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig, be backend.Backend, beExist bool, beHooks *serverstorage.BackendHooks, ci cindex.ConsistentIndexer) (*raftpb.Snapshot, backend.Backend, error) {\n\t// Find a snapshot to start/restart a raft node\n\twalSnaps, err := wal.ValidSnapshotEntries(cfg.Logger, cfg.WALDir())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, be, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot\n\tif len(walSnaps) > 0 {\n\t\tidx := len(walSnaps) - 1\n\t\tsnapshot = &raftpb.Snapshot{\n\t\t\tMetadata: raftpb.SnapshotMetadata{\n\t\t\t\tTerm:  walSnaps[idx].Term,\n\t\t\t\tIndex: walSnaps[idx].Index,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t}\n\t\tif walSnaps[idx].ConfState != nil {\n\t\t\tsnapshot.Metadata.ConfState = *walSnaps[idx].ConfState\n\t\t}\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"constructed a snapshot from WAL record\",\n\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"snapshot-index\", snapshot.Metadata.Index),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"snapshot-size\", humanize.Bytes(uint64(snapshot.Size()))),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"confState\", snapshot.Metadata.ConfState.String()),\n\t\t\tzap.Int(\"walSnaps-count\", len(walSnaps)),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\tif snapshot != nil {\n\t\tif be, err = serverstorage.RecoverSnapshotBackend(cfg, be, *snapshot, beExist, beHooks); err != nil {\n\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Panic(\"failed to recover v3 backend from snapshot\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t}\n\t\t// A snapshot db may have already been recovered, and the old db should have\n\t\t// already been closed in this case, so we should set the backend again.\n\t\tci.SetBackend(be)\n\n\t\tif beExist {\n\t\t\t// TODO: remove kvindex != 0 checking when we do not expect users to upgrade\n\t\t\t// etcd from pre-3.0 release.\n\t\t\tkvindex := ci.ConsistentIndex()\n\t\t\tif kvindex < snapshot.Metadata.Index {\n\t\t\t\tif kvindex != 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, be, fmt.Errorf(\"database file (%v index %d) does not match with snapshot (index %d)\", cfg.BackendPath(), kvindex, snapshot.Metadata.Index)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Warn(\n\t\t\t\t\t\"consistent index was never saved\",\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"snapshot-index\", snapshot.Metadata.Index),\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"No snapshot found. Recovering WAL from scratch!\")\n\t}\n\treturn snapshot, be, nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *bootstrappedCluster) Finalize(cfg config.ServerConfig, s *bootstrappedStorage) error {\n\tif !s.wal.haveWAL {\n\t\tc.cl.SetID(c.nodeID, c.cl.ID())\n\t}\n\tc.cl.SetBackend(schema.NewMembershipBackend(cfg.Logger, s.backend.be))\n\tif s.wal.haveWAL {\n\t\tc.cl.Recover(api.UpdateCapability)\n\t\tif c.databaseFileMissing(s) {\n\t\t\tbepath := cfg.BackendPath()\n\t\t\tos.RemoveAll(bepath)\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"database file (%v) of the backend is missing\", bepath)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tscaleUpLearners := false\n\treturn membership.ValidateMaxLearnerConfig(cfg.MaxLearners, c.cl.Members(), scaleUpLearners)\n}\n\nfunc (c *bootstrappedCluster) databaseFileMissing(s *bootstrappedStorage) bool {\n\tv3Cluster := c.cl.Version() != nil && !c.cl.Version().LessThan(semver.Version{Major: 3})\n\treturn v3Cluster && !s.backend.beExist\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapRaft(cfg config.ServerConfig, cluster *bootstrappedCluster, bwal *bootstrappedWAL) *bootstrappedRaft {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase !bwal.haveWAL && !cfg.NewCluster:\n\t\treturn bootstrapRaftFromCluster(cfg, cluster.cl, nil, bwal)\n\tcase !bwal.haveWAL && cfg.NewCluster:\n\t\treturn bootstrapRaftFromCluster(cfg, cluster.cl, cluster.cl.MemberIDs(), bwal)\n\tcase bwal.haveWAL:\n\t\treturn bootstrapRaftFromWAL(cfg, bwal)\n\tdefault:\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Panic(\"unsupported bootstrap config\")\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapRaftFromCluster(cfg config.ServerConfig, cl *membership.RaftCluster, ids []types.ID, bwal *bootstrappedWAL) *bootstrappedRaft {\n\tmember := cl.MemberByName(cfg.Name)\n\tpeers := make([]raft.Peer, len(ids))\n\tfor i, id := range ids {\n\t\tvar ctx []byte\n\t\tctx, err := json.Marshal((*cl).Member(id))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Panic(\"failed to marshal member\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t}\n\t\tpeers[i] = raft.Peer{ID: uint64(id), Context: ctx}\n\t}\n\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n\t\t\"starting local member\",\n\t\tzap.String(\"local-member-id\", member.ID.String()),\n\t\tzap.String(\"cluster-id\", cl.ID().String()),\n\t)\n\ts := bwal.MemoryStorage()\n\treturn &bootstrappedRaft{\n\t\tlg:        cfg.Logger,\n\t\theartbeat: time.Duration(cfg.TickMs) * time.Millisecond,\n\t\tconfig:    raftConfig(cfg, uint64(member.ID), s),\n\t\tpeers:     peers,\n\t\tstorage:   s,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapRaftFromWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, bwal *bootstrappedWAL) *bootstrappedRaft {\n\ts := bwal.MemoryStorage()\n\treturn &bootstrappedRaft{\n\t\tlg:        cfg.Logger,\n\t\theartbeat: time.Duration(cfg.TickMs) * time.Millisecond,\n\t\tconfig:    raftConfig(cfg, uint64(bwal.meta.nodeID), s),\n\t\tstorage:   s,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc raftConfig(cfg config.ServerConfig, id uint64, s *raft.MemoryStorage) *raft.Config {\n\treturn &raft.Config{\n\t\tID:              id,\n\t\tElectionTick:    cfg.ElectionTicks,\n\t\tHeartbeatTick:   1,\n\t\tStorage:         s,\n\t\tMaxSizePerMsg:   maxSizePerMsg,\n\t\tMaxInflightMsgs: maxInflightMsgs,\n\t\tCheckQuorum:     true,\n\t\tPreVote:         cfg.PreVote,\n\t\tLogger:          NewRaftLoggerZap(cfg.Logger.Named(\"raft\")),\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (b *bootstrappedRaft) newRaftNode(ss *snap.Snapshotter, wal *wal.WAL, cl *membership.RaftCluster) *raftNode {\n\tvar n raft.Node\n\tif len(b.peers) == 0 {\n\t\tn = raft.RestartNode(b.config)\n\t} else {\n\t\tn = raft.StartNode(b.config, b.peers)\n\t}\n\traftStatusMu.Lock()\n\traftStatus = n.Status\n\traftStatusMu.Unlock()\n\treturn newRaftNode(\n\t\traftNodeConfig{\n\t\t\tlg:          b.lg,\n\t\t\tisIDRemoved: func(id uint64) bool { return cl.IsIDRemoved(types.ID(id)) },\n\t\t\tNode:        n,\n\t\t\theartbeat:   b.heartbeat,\n\t\t\traftStorage: b.storage,\n\t\t\tstorage:     serverstorage.NewStorage(b.lg, wal, ss),\n\t\t},\n\t)\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapWALFromSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig, snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot, ci cindex.ConsistentIndexer) *bootstrappedWAL {\n\twal, st, ents, snap, meta := openWALFromSnapshot(cfg, snapshot)\n\tbwal := &bootstrappedWAL{\n\t\tlg:       cfg.Logger,\n\t\tw:        wal,\n\t\tst:       st,\n\t\tents:     ents,\n\t\tsnapshot: snap,\n\t\tmeta:     meta,\n\t\thaveWAL:  true,\n\t}\n\n\tif cfg.ForceNewCluster {\n\t\tconsistentIndex := ci.ConsistentIndex()\n\t\toldCommitIndex := bwal.st.Commit\n\t\t// If only `HardState.Commit` increases, HardState won't be persisted\n\t\t// to disk, even though the committed entries might have already been\n\t\t// applied. This can result in consistent_index > CommitIndex.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// When restarting etcd with `--force-new-cluster`, all uncommitted\n\t\t// entries are dropped. To avoid losing entries that were actually\n\t\t// committed, we reset Commit to max(HardState.Commit, consistent_index).\n\t\t//\n\t\t// See: https://github.com/etcd-io/raft/pull/300 for more details.\n\t\tbwal.st.Commit = max(oldCommitIndex, consistentIndex)\n\n\t\t// discard the previously uncommitted entries\n\t\tbwal.ents = bwal.CommitedEntries()\n\t\tentries := bwal.NewConfigChangeEntries()\n\t\t// force commit config change entries\n\t\tbwal.AppendAndCommitEntries(entries)\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\"forcing restart member\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"cluster-id\", meta.clusterID.String()),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"local-member-id\", meta.nodeID.String()),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"wal-commit-index\", oldCommitIndex),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"commit-index\", bwal.st.Commit),\n\t\t)\n\t} else {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\"restarting local member\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"cluster-id\", meta.clusterID.String()),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"local-member-id\", meta.nodeID.String()),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"commit-index\", bwal.st.Commit),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn bwal\n}\n\n// openWALFromSnapshot reads the WAL at the given snap and returns the wal, its latest HardState and cluster ID, and all entries that appear\n// after the position of the given snap in the WAL.\n// The snap must have been previously saved to the WAL, or this call will panic.\nfunc openWALFromSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig, snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot) (*wal.WAL, *raftpb.HardState, []raftpb.Entry, *raftpb.Snapshot, *snapshotMetadata) {\n\tvar walsnap walpb.Snapshot\n\tif snapshot != nil {\n\t\twalsnap.Index, walsnap.Term = snapshot.Metadata.Index, snapshot.Metadata.Term\n\t}\n\trepaired := false\n\tfor {\n\t\tw, err := wal.Open(cfg.Logger, cfg.WALDir(), walsnap)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\"failed to open WAL\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t}\n\t\tif cfg.UnsafeNoFsync {\n\t\t\tw.SetUnsafeNoFsync()\n\t\t}\n\t\twmetadata, st, ents, err := w.ReadAll()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tw.Close()\n\t\t\t// we can only repair ErrUnexpectedEOF and we never repair twice.\n\t\t\tif repaired || !errors.Is(err, io.ErrUnexpectedEOF) {\n\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\"failed to read WAL, cannot be repaired\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif !wal.Repair(cfg.Logger, cfg.WALDir()) {\n\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\"failed to repair WAL\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\"repaired WAL\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t\trepaired = true\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tvar metadata etcdserverpb.Metadata\n\t\tpbutil.MustUnmarshal(&metadata, wmetadata)\n\t\tid := types.ID(metadata.NodeID)\n\t\tcid := config.ServerConfig, snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot, ci cindex.ConsistentIndexer) *bootstrappedWAL {\n\twal, st, ents, snap, meta := openWALFromSnapshot(cfg, snapshot)\n\tbwal := &bootstrappedWAL{\n\t\tlg:       cfg.Logger,\n\t\tw:        wal,\n\t\tst:       st,\n\t\tents:     ents,\n\t\tsnapshot: snap,\n\t\tmeta:     meta,\n\t\thaveWAL:  true,\n\t}\n\n\tif cfg.ForceNewCluster {\n\t\tconsistentIndex := ci.ConsistentIndex()\n\t\toldCommitIndex := bwal.st.Commit\n\t\t// If only `HardState.Commit` increases, HardState won't be persisted\n\t\t// to disk, even though the committed entries might have already been\n\t\t// applied. This can result in consistent_index > CommitIndex.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// When restarting etcd with `--force-new-cluster`, all uncommitted\n\t\t// entries are dropped. To avoid losing entries that were actually\n\t\t// committed, we reset Commit to max(HardState.Commit, consistent_index).\n\t\t//\n\t\t// See: https://github.com/etcd-io/raft/pull/300 for more details.\n\t\tbwal.st.Commit = max(oldCommitIndex, consistentIndex)\n\n\t\t// discard the previously uncommitted entries\n\t\tbwal.ents = bwal.CommitedEntries()\n\t\tentries := bwal.NewConfigChangeEntries()\n\t\t// force commit config change entries\n\t\tbwal.AppendAndCommitEntries(entries)\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\"forcing restart oldCommitIndex),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"commit-index\", bwal.st.Commit),\n\t\t)\n\t} else {\n\t\tcfg.Logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\"restarting local member\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"cluster-id\", meta.clusterID.String()),\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"local-member-id\", meta.nodeID.String()),\n\t\t\tzap.Uint64(\"commit-index\", bwal.st.Commit),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn bwal\n}\n\n// openWALFromSnapshot reads the WAL at the given snap and returns the wal, its latest HardState and cluster ID, and all entries that appear\n// after the position of the given snap in the WAL.\n// The snap must have been previously saved to the WAL, or this call will panic.\nfunc openWALFromSnapshot(cfg config.ServerConfig, snapshot *raftpb.Snapshot) (*wal.WAL, *raftpb.HardState, []raftpb.Entry, *raftpb.Snapshot, *snapshotMetadata) {\n\tvar walsnap walpb.Snapshot\n\tif snapshot != nil {\n\t\twalsnap.Index, walsnap.Term = snapshot.Metadata.Index, snapshot.Metadata.Term\n\t}\n\trepaired := false\n\tfor {\n\t\tw, {\n\t\t\tw.SetUnsafeNoFsync()\n\t\t}\n\t\twmetadata, st, ents, err := w.ReadAll()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tw.Close()\n\t\t\t// we can only repair ErrUnexpectedEOF and we never repair twice.\n\t\t\tif repaired || !errors.Is(err, io.ErrUnexpectedEOF) {\n\t\t\t\tcfg.Logger.Fatal(\"failed to read WAL, cannot be repaired\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif !wal.Repair(cfg.Logger, true\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tvar metadata etcdserverpb.Metadata\n\t\tpbutil.MustUnmarshal(&metadata, wmetadata)\n\t\tid := types.ID(metadata.NodeID)\n\t\tcid := types.ID(metadata.ClusterID)\n\t\tmeta := &snapshotMetadata{clusterID: cid, nodeID: id}\n\t\treturn w, &st, ents, snapshot, meta\n\t}\n}\n\ntype snapshotMetadata struct {\n\tnodeID, clusterID types.ID\n}\n\nfunc bootstrapNewWAL(cfg config.ServerConfig, cl *bootstrappedCluster) *bootstrappedWAL {\n\tmetadata := pbutil.MustMarshal(\n\t\t&etcdserverpb.Metadata{\n\t\t\tNodeID: *bootstrappedWAL) MemoryStorage() *raft.MemoryStorage {\n\ts := raft.NewMemoryStorage()\n\tif wal.snapshot != nil {\n\t\ts.ApplySnapshot(*wal.snapshot)\n\t}\n\tif wal.st != nil   features.NewDefaultServerFeatureGate(\"test\", lg),\n\t\t},\n\t\tr:                 *r,\n\t\tsnapshotter:       snap.New(lg, testdir),\n\t\tcluster:           cl,\n\t\tconsistIndex: uberApplierMock{},\n\t\tauthStore:         auth.NewAuthStore(lg, schema.NewAuthBackend(lg, be), nil, 1),\n\t}\n\n\ts.kv = mvcc.New(lg, be, &lease.FakeLessor{}, mvcc.StoreConfig{})\n\ts.be = be\n\n\ts.start()\n\tdefer s.Stop()\n\n\t// submit applied entries and snap entries\n\tidx := uint64(0)\n\toutdated := 0\n\taccepted := 0\n\tfor k := 1; k <= 101; k++ {\n\t\tidx++\n\t\tch := s.w.Register(idx)\n\t\treq := &pb.InternalRaftRequest{\n\t\t\tHeader: &pb.RequestHeader{ID: idx},\n\t\t\tPut:    &pb.PutRequest{Key: []byte(\"foo\"), Value: []byte(\"bar\")},\n\t\t}\n\t\tent := raftpb.Entry{Index: idx, Data: pbutil.MustMarshal(req)}\n\t\tready := raft.Ready{Entries: []raftpb.Entry{ent}}\n\t\tn.readyc <- ready\n\n\t\tready = raft.Ready{CommittedEntries: []raftpb.Entry{ent}}\n\t\tn.readyc <- ready\n\n\t\t// \"idx\" applied\n\t\t<-ch\n\n\t\t// one snapshot for every two messages\n\t\tif k%2 != 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tn.readyc <- raft.Ready{Messages: []raftpb.Message{{Type: raftpb.MsgSnap}}}\n\t\t// get the snapshot sent by the transport\n\t\tsnapMsg := <-snapDoneC\n\t\t// If the snapshot trails applied records, recovery will panic\n\t\t// since there's no allocated snapshot at the place of the\n\t\t// snapshot record. This only happens when the applier and the\n\t\t// snapshot sender get out of sync.\n\t\tif snapMsg.Snapshot.Metadata.Index == idx {\n\t\t\tidx++\n\t\t\tsnapMsg.Snapshot.Metadata.Index = idx\n\t\t\tready = raft.Ready{Snapshot: *snapMsg.Snapshot}\n\t\t\tn.readyc <- ready\n\t\t\taccepted++\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\toutdated++\n\t\t}\n\t\t// don't wait for the snapshot to complete, move to next message\n\t}\n\tif accepted != 50 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"accepted=%v, want 50\", accepted)\n\t}\n\tif outdated != 0 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"outdated=%v, want 0\", outdated)\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestAddMember tests
